[2;36m                    [0m         [39m== libFuzzer crashing input ==[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m===Evaluation [0m[33mReport[0m[39m===[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA Jazzer-based fuzzing session triggered a `FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical` exception [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mindicating a file path traversal vulnerability. The sanitizer detected an attempt [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto escape a target directory through “..[0m[35m/[0m[39m” segments when expanding archive entries [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvia the `Expander.expand` method in the Apache Commons Compress examples.[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Issue Type  [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  The issue is a file path traversal vulnerability, as reported by the Jazzer [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`FilePathTraversal` sanitizer.[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- What Happened  [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  During fuzz testing, a crafted input caused the `Expander.expand` routine to [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprocess a path containing “..[0m[35m/../[0m[95mjazzer-traversal[0m[39m” relative to a temporary [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdirectory. The sanitizer’s `check` and `checkPath` methods flagged this as an [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munauthorized upward directory traversal and raised a `FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical` [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexception.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Key Observations  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The exception originates in [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`com.code_intelligence.jazzer.sanitizers.FilePathTraversal`, specifically in the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmethods `check`, `checkPath`, and `pathFirstArgHook`.  [0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The vulnerable code path is exercised by the `Expander.expand` calls in [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`org.apache.commons.compress.archivers.examples.Expander`. The stack trace shows [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmultiple overloads of `expand` leading into the sanitation hook.  [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The fuzzer harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`ExpanderFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is merely the entry [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpoint for delivering the malicious input to `Expander`; it is not the root cause.[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Code Areas for Investigation  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. `com.code_intelligence.jazzer.sanitizers.FilePathTraversal`  [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     – Methods: `[0m[1;35mcheck[0m[1;39m([0m[39mPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, `[0m[1;35mcheckPath[0m[1;39m([0m[39mPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, `[0m[1;35mpathFirstArgHook[0m[1;39m([0m[39mObject, Method,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mObject[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`  [0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. `org.apache.commons.compress.archivers.examples.Expander`  [0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     – Overloaded `expand` methods around lines [0m[1;36m86[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m204[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m324[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m400[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m460[0m[39m of [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`Expander.java`  [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. The interaction between the archive-entry processing logic in `Expander` and [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpath normalization/validation steps.[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA holistic review of how `Expander` handles output paths, how it normalizes or [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msanitizes archive entry names, and how the Jazzer sanitizer hooks into file-path [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39marguments will be necessary to fully understand the vulnerability surface.[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Initial Issue Log[0m                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msrc/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/archivers/ArchiveEntry.jav[0m[1;92ma:78[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m89[0m         [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m78[0m[39m:    default Path [0m[1;35mresolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mfinal Path parentPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m throws IOException [0m[1;39m{[0m           [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mStandardCharsets.US_ASCII.name[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                 [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause Analysis[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The vulnerability resides in the default `[0m[1;35mresolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mPath parentPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mimplementation in `ArchiveEntry.java`.  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The method currently:[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     a[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Resolves the raw entry name and normalizes it, then enforces a “zip-slip” [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcheck.  [0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     b[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Discards that safe, normalized result and instead returns a fresh [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mparentPath.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdecodedName[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` *without* normalization.  [0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - A malicious entry name containing percent-encoded “..[0m[35m/[0m[39m” [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g. [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m“..%2F..%2Ffile”[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m bypasses the initial check once decoded, because no subsequent [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnormalization is applied.[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   A. Reorder and consolidate decoding, normalization, and checking into a single [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstep.  [0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   B. Steps to implement in [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`src/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/archivers/ArchiveEntry.java`:[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. Remove the two-stage resolution [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnormalize raw, then re-resolve decoded[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. First URL-decode the entry name, falling back to the raw name on decode [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39merrors.  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Perform a single `[0m[1;35mresolve[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdecodedName[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.  [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Apply the `[0m[1;35mstartsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mparentPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` check on the normalized result.  [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m. Return the normalized, validated path.[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   C. Preserve existing behavior:[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Continuously support percent-decoded names for entries.[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Fallback to raw names if decoding fails.[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Throw `IOException` on any detected path traversal.[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   D. No changes to fuzz-harness code, test code, or external dependencies.[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Detailed Implementation Outline[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   In `ArchiveEntry.java`, replace the `resolveIn` default method [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines ~[0m[1;36m78[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m89[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwith:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   default Path [0m[1;35mresolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mPath parentPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m throws IOException [0m[1;39m{[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       final String name = [0m[1;35mgetName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       final String decodedName;[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       try [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           decodedName = [0m[1;35mURLDecoder.decode[0m[1;39m([0m[39mname, [0m[1;35mStandardCharsets.US_ASCII.name[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m catch [0m[1;39m([0m[39mIllegalArgumentException | UnsupportedEncodingException e[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Fallback: use raw name if decoding fails[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           decodedName = name;[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Normalize after decoding[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       final Path outputFile = [0m[1;35mparentPath.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdecodedName[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35moutputFile.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mparentPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m               [0m[1;35mString.format[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Zip slip '%s' + '%s' -> '%s'"[0m[39m, parentPath, [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdecodedName, outputFile[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           [0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       return outputFile;[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This single-pass approach ensures no “..[0m[35m/[0m[39m” segments survive without [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnormalization.[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The `startsWith` check is applied against the decoding result, so malicious [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdecoded paths are caught.[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Justification[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Security**: Eliminates the window where decoded “..[0m[35m/[0m[39m” can bypass [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnormalization.[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Compatibility**: Maintains current decoding support and [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexception‐on‐traversal behavior.[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Minimal Impact**: Touches only one method; does not alter public APIs or [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtest/harness code.[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Precedent**: Many archive-processing libraries decode first, then normalize,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthen validate [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., OWASP zip-slip mitigations[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Testing & Side Effects[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Add unit tests for entries with mixed raw and percent-encoded “..[0m[35m/[0m[39m” to ensure [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`IOException` is thrown.[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Verify existing examples and archives with legitimate percent-encoded names [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstill unpack correctly.[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No side effects expected outside of improved security on entry path [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mresolution.[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         ## Summary                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         The initial issue is a Jazzer-detected security crash: a                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical` is thrown for a file path traversal when the          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `Expander` example attempts to write entries outside of its target directory. The   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         user’s patch modifies the `[1;35mArchiveEntry.resolveIn[0m[1m([0mPath[1m)[0m` default implementation by  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         URL-decoding the entry name before resolving and normalizing it, updating the error [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         message accordingly, and removing the old decoding logic. After applying the patch, [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         the Maven build fails with a compilation error in `ArchiveEntry.java` citing that   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         the local variable `decodedName` “might already have been assigned.”                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Description                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         Initial Issue                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - The fuzzer triggers a critical Jazzer exception:                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           `com.code_intelligence.jazzer.api.FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical: File path          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         traversal: [35m/tmp/[0m…[35m/../../[0m[95mjazzer-traversal[0m`.                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - The sanitizer stack trace shows the failure occurring in:                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1;36m1[0m. `FilePathTraversal.check`                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1;36m2[0m. `FilePathTraversal.checkPath`                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1;36m3[0m. `FilePathTraversal.pathFirstArgHook`                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1;36m4[0m. `[1;35mExpander.expand[0m[1m([0m[33m...[0m[1m)[0m`                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1;36m5[0m. `[1;35mExpanderFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput[0m[1m([0mExpanderFuzzer.jav[1;92ma:52[0m[1m)[0m`                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - This indicates that an archive entry with a name containing `..` allowed          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         directory-escaping past the intended extraction root.                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         Patch Attempt                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Edited `ArchiveEntry.java`, method `[1;35mresolveIn[0m[1m([0mfinal Path parentPath[1m)[0m`:            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           • Introduced a `decodedName` string, assigned via `[1;35mURLDecoder.decode[0m[1m([0mname,        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         US_ASCII[1m)[0m`, with a catch block falling back to the raw `name`.                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           • Changed resolution to `[1;35mparentPath.resolve[0m[1m([0mdecodedName[1m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m` and updated [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         the zip-slip exception message to include `decodedName`.                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           • Removed the original post-normalization decoding logic.                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - The diff context at lines ~[1;36m77[0m–[1;36m96[0m in `ArchiveEntry.java` shows both the            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         declaration of `decodedName` and its use in path resolution and exception           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         formatting.                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         Patch Result                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - The Maven compile phase reports a single error in `ArchiveEntry.java` at line [1;36m85[0m: [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         compiler plugin step.                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - No runtime or sanitizer logs beyond the compile failure are produced, indicating  [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mStandardCharsets.US_ASCII.name[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m86[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m catch [0m[1;39m([0m[39mIllegalArgumentException | UnsupportedEncodingException e[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m87[0m[39m:            return outputFile;[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m88[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m89[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause Analysis  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The compilation error “variable decodedName might already have been assigned” [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39marises because the blank `final String decodedName;` is assigned in both the `try` [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand the `catch` blocks. Although Java’s definite‐assignment rules theoretically [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallow exactly one assignment per control path, in practice the compiler is unable [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto verify that the two assignments never occur in the same execution path, and thus[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrejects the code.  [0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Beyond the compile error, the prior implementation had a two‐step [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnormalization/decode logic that allowed a decoded name to bypass the zip‐slip [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcheck. The correct security fix is to decode the entry name first, then do a single[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mresolve/normalize/check on the decoded name.[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Key Constraints and Goals  [0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Preserve the existing API: `[0m[1;35mArchiveEntry.resolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` remains a `default` [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minterface method.  [0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Maintain correct behavior for entries that do not require decoding [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfallback [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto raw name[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Do not modify fuzz harness code, tests, or external libraries.  [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Ensure a single decode → normalize → zip‐slip‐check → return sequence.  [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Eliminate the compile‐time definite‐assignment error by simplifying [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`decodedName` handling.[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Proposed Patch Workflow  [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. In `src/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/archivers/ArchiveEntry.java`, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreplace the body of the `[0m[1;35mresolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mPath parentPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` default method with the [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfollowing logic:  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Declare a non‐final local `String decodedName` initialized to the raw entry[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mname.  [0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - In a `try` block, attempt to URL‐decode UTF‐[0m[1;36m8[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mUS‐ASCII[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m the raw name; on [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msuccess, overwrite `decodedName`.  [0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - In the `catch` block, simply swallow the exception [0m[1;39m([0m[39mleaving `decodedName` [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mas the raw name[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Resolve and then normalize `decodedName` against `parentPath`.  [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - If the resulting path does not start with `parentPath`, throw an [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`IOException` containing the decoded name.  [0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Return the normalized, checked `Path`.  [0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Remove all other normalization or decode logic in this method so there is [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexactly one pass of normalize/check on the decoded name.  [0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Detailed Steps  [0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. Open `ArchiveEntry.java`.  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Locate the `default Path [0m[1;35mresolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mfinal Path parentPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m throws IOException`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmethod [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround line [0m[1;36m78[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Replace its entire existing body with:[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```java[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      default Path [0m[1;35mresolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mfinal Path parentPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m throws IOException [0m[1;39m{[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Get raw entry name.[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          final String rawName = [0m[1;35mgetName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Decode once, fallback to rawName.[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          String decodedName = rawName;[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          try [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              decodedName = [0m[1;35mURLDecoder.decode[0m[1;39m([0m[39mrawName, [0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mStandardCharsets.US_ASCII.name[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m catch [0m[1;39m([0m[39mIllegalArgumentException | UnsupportedEncodingException e[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m ignore: keep decodedName == rawName[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[1;36m3[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Resolve & normalize the decoded name.[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          final Path target = [0m[1;35mparentPath.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdecodedName[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[1;36m4[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Zip‐slip check.[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mtarget.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mparentPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                  [0m[1;35mString.format[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Zip slip '%s' + '%s' -> '%s'"[0m[39m, parentPath, [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdecodedName, target[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[1;36m5[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Safe to return.[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          return target;[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Ensure imports remain:[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```java[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      import java.io.IOException;[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      import java.io.UnsupportedEncodingException;[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      import java.net.URLDecoder;[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      import java.nio.charset.StandardCharsets;[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      import java.nio.file.Path;[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Justification  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - By initializing `decodedName` to `rawName`, we eliminate any ambiguous “might [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39malready have been assigned” cases and remove the need for a blank final.  [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - All code paths now follow a clear decode‐first then normalize/check pattern, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mclosing the zip‐slip vulnerability.  [0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No existing tests or harnesses need modification; the public method signature [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand its intended functionality remain consistent.  [0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This approach mirrors the recommended single‐pass normalization strategy in [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe Commons Compress codebase and aligns with secure file‐extraction best [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpractices.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Potential Side Effects & Mitigations  [0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - If future code migrates to a different character set, the [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`StandardCharsets.US_ASCII` parameter may need review, but that matches the [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpreexisting choice.  [0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Overly broad `catch` for `IllegalArgumentException` safely falls back to the [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mraw name, preserving backward compatibility.  [0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No additional side effects are anticipated, as no other code relies on the old[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtwo‐step approach.[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. Verification  [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Rebuild the project with `mvn package` to confirm the compilation error is [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mresolved.  [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Run existing unit and integration tests to ensure no regressions.  [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Execute the ExpanderFuzzer again to verify that path‐traversal inputs now [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtrigger the intended `IOException` in the zip‐slip guard.  [0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
